
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Analyze the properties of the convex equilateral hexagon with opposite sides parallel to establish geometric constraints.'}, {'objective': "Determine the relationship between the hexagon's sides and the sides of the triangle formed by the extensions of segments AB, CD, and EF."}, {'objective': 'Express the side length of the hexagon in terms of the given triangle side lengths using the parallelism and equilateral conditions.'}, {'objective': "Set up and solve the resulting equations to find the hexagon's side length."}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The figure is a convex equilateral hexagon ABCDEF.
- All pairs of opposite sides are parallel, implying ABCDEF is a parallelogon with three pairs of parallel sides.
- The hexagon is equilateral, so all six sides have the same length, say s.
- The triangle formed by the extensions of sides AB, CD, and EF has side lengths 200, 240, and 300.
- The objective is to find the side length s of the hexagon.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- Since ABCDEF is convex, equilateral, and has opposite sides parallel, it is a special type of hexagon often called an affine-regular hexagon or a hexagon with translational symmetry.
- The three pairs of opposite sides being parallel means AB ∥ DE, BC ∥ EF, and CD ∥ FA.
- The triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF suggests these lines intersect pairwise outside the hexagon, forming a triangle whose sides correspond to the distances between these intersection points.
- The side lengths 200, 240, and 300 of this triangle relate to the directions and lengths of the hexagon’s sides, possibly through vector addition or geometric transformations.
- The problem likely involves relating the hexagon’s side length s to the given triangle side lengths via geometric or vector properties.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in Euclidean geometry, specifically polygon geometry and properties of convex polygons.
- It involves concepts from affine geometry (parallelism, equilateral polygons), vector geometry (side vectors), and possibly triangle inequalities.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and advanced geometry studies.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The exact construction of the triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF is not explicitly described; it is assumed that the lines containing these sides intersect pairwise to form a triangle.
- The orientation and labeling of the hexagon’s vertices are not specified, which might affect vector directions.
- It is assumed the hexagon is strictly convex and equilateral with the stated parallelism, but no explicit coordinate system or angle measures are given.
- To proceed, one might assume standard orientation or use vector methods to express side directions and lengths, relating them to the triangle’s side lengths.

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Identify and verify the geometric elements and constraints of the problem. "
        "Confirm that ABCDEF is a convex equilateral hexagon with three pairs of opposite sides parallel (AB ∥ DE, BC ∥ EF, CD ∥ FA), "
        "and that all sides have equal length s. Establish notation for side vectors and their directions, and clarify the construction of the triangle formed by the extensions of sides AB, CD, and EF. "
        "Avoid assuming any coordinate system prematurely; focus on properties implied by the problem statement and parallelism conditions."
    )
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, analyzing geometric elements and constraints, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2: Formulate the vector representation of the hexagon's sides based on the parallelism and equilateral conditions. "
        "Assign vectors to sides AB, BC, CD, DE, EF, and FA such that opposite sides are parallel and equal in length. "
        "Verify that the sum of the six side vectors is zero (closed polygon condition). "
        "This sets the foundation for relating the hexagon's side length to the triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF."
    )
    N = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_2 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_2 = []
    possible_thinkings_2 = []
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1, answer1],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agents_2[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], cot_sc_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_2[i].id}, formulating vector representation, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
        possible_answers_2.append(answer2)
        possible_thinkings_2.append(thinking2)
    final_decision_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking2, answer2 = await final_decision_agent_2([taskInfo] + possible_answers_2 + possible_thinkings_2, "Sub-task 2: Synthesize and choose the most consistent vector representation solution." , is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking2, "answer": answer2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_3 = (
        "Sub-task 3: Determine the directions and relative orientations of the vectors corresponding to sides AB, CD, and EF, "
        "and analyze how their extensions intersect to form the triangle with side lengths 200, 240, and 300. "
        "Use vector geometry to express the sides of this triangle in terms of the hexagon's side length s and the directions of AB, CD, and EF. "
        "Enumerate all valid vector combinations and angle relationships that satisfy the parallelism and convexity constraints."
    )
    cot_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_3 = []
    possible_thinkings_3 = []
    subtask_desc3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",

    cot_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc4 = {
